💭 _“Always look at the solution, not the problem. Learn to focus on what will give results.”_ 💭 

_*TECHNOCRAT '21*_, a state-level technical symposium under *EESA* i.e. _Electrical Engineering Students' Association_ club of WCE, Sangli presents 

           🗣 _*Walchand MUN*_ 🗣
                 - Voice of people🎙️

🍁Walchand MUN is an event which stands for Model United Nations, where you all will come to the event as delegates of various nations to participate and debate. Finally, after the conference, you come out of the event as an enlightened person.🍁 

This event has 3 rounds
🎯 *ROUND 1- Report Submission*📄
Submission of report on given problem statement. 

🎯 *ROUND 2- Presenting the solutions*🧠
Round will consist of presenting the solutions on the given problem statement, debate & cross-questioning.  

🎯 *ROUND 3- Surprise round*🎁 

Why should I  participate in *Walchand MUN*? 

-MUN is not just about gaining knowledge, but improving your weak areas, developing interpersonal communication, and being able to speak confidently in public. Also, it helps in networking & gaining leadership skills. 

💥It's an amazing opportunity to take a break from your monotonous routine and to  engage with your peers and learn something new & exciting.💥 

🔅No. Of participants/team- *2* 
🔅Entry Fees- *Rs 20*
🔅Event Date- *6th June*
🔅To register, visit EESA's website: http://wceeesa.org.in/

- There is a volcano on Mars three times the size of Everest -- Olympus Mons🌋

- The Moon was once a piece of the Earth.🌕

- There is floating water in space -- Astronomers have found a massive water vapor cloud which holds 140 trillion times the mass of water in the Earth’s oceans somewhere around 10 billion light years away – making it the largest discovery of water ever found.☁☁

- Most of the stuff in the Universe has repulsive gravity -- this is also the reason why universe expansion is speeding up

- It rains diamonds on Jupiter and Saturn -- chunks of Graphite which then turn into diamonds💎💎

12/13/21, 17:49 - Devang Wce: WCE GDSC and Dept. of CSE presents "The Intra CSE Hackathon".

As a part of the celebration of “Bharat ki Azadi ka Amrut Mahotsav”, Directorate of Technical
Education, Maharashtra State has decided to conduct technical activities.
In this connection, the Regional Office, Directorate of Technical Education, Pune in
association with VIT, Pune is organizing the Regional Level Project Competition.

Process:
1. Every student from 1st to 4th year can participate in a team of 2-4.
2. You can submit your already made projects with a description in the following form.
3. Shortlisted teams will give a presentation to the department panel.
4. The last date to apply is 13 Dec 2021.
5. Top 15 teams get a chance to exhibit in ACM RSC.
6. 1st Qualifies as the entry from our campus for the finals in VIT Pune(Online).

Form Link: https://forms.gle/1ggkRMaEgrrJB2aS7

Regards,
GDSC.

1/5/22, 12:48 - Rutikesh Wal: Greetings!
 
We, the students of the Indian Institute of Science Education and Research (IISER) Pune are pleased to announce the fourteenth edition of our annual national-level science challenge, *Mimamsa*, a science challenge like no other in India- organized entirely by students of IISER Pune.

This year, Mimamsa would be held in a two-stage format.

College students who are in the *first three years of Undergraduate education get to form a team of 3 or 4 participants* and compete in the first stage, dubbed the ‘Prelims’, to be held online, in February. The Top 4 teams across the country would then compete in the second and final stage ‘Mains’, which is held on IISER-Pune campus and is scheduled to be held in April.
 
Mimamsa 2022 *Prelims is scheduled to be held on 20th February (Sunday) 2022 from 10 AM to 12 AM*. It will be an online test of both objective and subjective questions comprising 4 sections (Physics, Chemistry, Mathematics and Biology).
 
Registrations are now open. There is no exam fee. *The last date for registration is 13th Febuary 2022*.

There are *prizes worth ₹2,00,000 along with other cool prizes for zonal and subject toppers*. Add to this the honour of representing one’s college at a renowned national level Science challenge.
 
For registration, please visit http://mimamsa.iiserpune.ac.in. Further information can be found on the same. In case of any queries, please feel free to write to us at mimamsa@sac.iiserpune.ac.in, or contact the campus coordinator whose contact details are given below. 

Warm regards,
Team Mimamsa 2022

For queries, contact:
Prajakta

🔸 *GECA MUN* is an initiative of the students of *Government College of Engineering, Aurangabad* that works on the motto *"Engage, Encourage, Empower"* and provides a platform for the youth to showcase their concerns of national and international interests.

✨ *Warm Rotaract Greetings!!*✨

💫 *Without change there is no innovation, creativity and incentive for improvement. And the greatest device for those is a curious mind.* 💫

With this intent, Rotaract Club of WCE Sangli presents *Megaevent 2022* under International Service Avenue *"GLOBAL MANDATE - Global Quest for Noble Cause"*🔥

Participants will get acquainted with the purpose of *Model United Nations,* i.e., to provide an interactive educational experience that teaches an interesting and enjoyable way about the United Nations. The process affords participants, an understanding of how the process of *international debate* and *negotiation* that we commonly call diplomacy, actually functions.🧐

⭕ *Key takeaways:*
📍Public Speaking🎙️
📍Perception of Global Issues📰 
📍Enhance Directorship ✅ 
📍Superintending ability🎯

Round 1️⃣ - 30 min
Round 2️⃣-  3 hrs 
Round 3️⃣ -  30 min
Mode: Fully Online.

🔖What is the total time for the DevelopZilla Event?

The total time will be approximately 4 hours. And participants will have some short breaks in between rounds.

🔖What technologies the participants can use?

Participants can use any technology with which they are comfortable. Generic problem statements will be given and participants can implement them either in web or mobile applications.

🔖Type of problem statements.

There will be two groups one is a novice and the other is an expert. Novice will have problem statements based on frontend only and experts will have problem statements based on both frontend and backend. Price distribution will be according to the category participants have chosen. Experts will have a higher price than novices. And both types of participants will be judged independently and individually. 

🔖Rounds:
1. Aptitude.
2. Implementation based on the problem statement.
3. The third round will be a presentation of the second round and each member has to present the website or web application or mobile application.

🔖Problem Statement (Example):
	Design a website or web app or mobile application for a Shopping mall billing system.

Following are some guidelines / instructions for smooth running of online examination.

1. Update the web browser with latest version.

2. Login the examination immediately after the link has enabled. Requests for login after 10: 35 am won't be addressed.

3. The routine excuses by students such as poor network, weak bandwidth , power failure, exhaust of data will not be entertained at all. 

4. It is customary to report query on telegram platform only, most of the time problem arises due to poor network only hence find healthy network place to get rid of the query, do not flood up the inbox with messeges otherwise appear the examination through institute , we will provide all necessary amenities in the premises. 

5. The examination duration includes uploading time hence upload the images accordingly to avoid last minute burdon.

6. Examination link will be disabled at scheduled time irrespective of your login time expect for PWD students. The browser will be disabled automatically saving all your answers and images hence do not post the messages  asking for its acknowledgments.

7. Most of the students appear examination through android devices, we will encourage to use desktops with ups or full battery charged laptops.


8. The examination controller, students and proctoring agency are monitoring the examination remotely from different places hence judicious and ethical behaviour along with healthy cooperation is expected from students.


9. Lastly, in highly emergency situation connect with DCOE of respective departments only throgh mail or voice call. Refer attached pdf containing connect details.


B N Naik
